021|4. As a seller, I want to receive notifications about new orders so that I can fulfill them promptly.
022|5. As a driver, I want to receive delivery status updates so that I can manage my deliveries effectively.

001|# AI-Powered Ordering System PRD
002|
003|## Project Name
004|ai_powered_ordering_system
005|
006|## Language
007|English
008|
009|## Restated Requirements
010|Create an AI-powered ordering system where customers can manage personalized product lists, place orders using a one-click or natural language input, while sellers and drivers manage order fulfillment and delivery status updates, with notifications for all parties involved.
011|
012|## Product Goals
013|1. Enable customers to create and manage personalized product lists efficiently.
014|2. Facilitate seamless order placement through one-click and natural language input.
015|3. Provide real-time order fulfillment and delivery status updates for sellers and drivers.
016|
017|## User Stories
018|1. As a customer, I want to create a personalized product list so that I can easily manage my favorite items.
019|2. As a customer, I want to place an order with one click so that I can save time during the checkout process.
020|3. As a customer, I want to use natural language input to place orders so that I can interact with the system more intuitively.
021|4. As a seller, I want to receive notifications about new orders so that I can fulfill them promptly.
022|5. As a driver, I want to receive delivery status updates so that I can manage my deliveries effectively.
